## What changed

### `vega-chart.tsx` (production)
- Added `useState<string | null>` for `error`.
- `setError(null)` at start of each `useEffect` invocation (clear stale; per Codex iter-2 P2).
- `.catch` block now calls `setError(...)` only when `!cancelled` (avoid post-unmount state update).
- Render a sibling `<div data-testid="vega-chart-error" role="alert">` ABOVE the mount div when `error !== null`. Mount div remains permanently in JSX so future spec changes can re-trigger embed.
- Added `data-testid="vega-chart"` to mount div for Playwright.
- Existing API (`spec`, `className`, `onPointClick`) preserved unchanged → existing inspector consumer at `web/app/inspector/[runId]/page.tsx` continues to work without source modification.

### `charts_test/page.tsx` (NEW demo route)
- Hand-authored Vega-Lite v5 sample spec: `$schema` v5 URL; bar chart of 3 data points (POLARIS / ChatGPT DR / Gemini DR scores on "Sourcing" dimension); `width`/`height` set in spec; `polaris_provenance: { chart_type: "forest_plot", evidence_ids: ["demo-1","demo-2","demo-3"] }` (per `VegaLiteSpec` contract; "forest_plot" is one of the 3 valid `ChartType` values).
- Honest-frame copy explains "demo evidence_ids only; consumed by real forest-plot in I-f10-002."

### `vega_lite_chart.spec.ts` (Playwright)
- Visit `/charts_test`, assert `[data-testid="vega-chart"]` visible, wait for `svg` to attach (≤10s), assert `svg path` count > 0 (Vega rect marks are SVG paths per Codex iter-1 P1 verification), assert no `[data-testid="vega-chart-error"]`.

## Risks for Codex Red-Team

1. **API back-compat:** `VegaChart` props unchanged (`spec`, `className`, `onPointClick`). Existing inspector consumer (`web/app/inspector/[runId]/page.tsx`) compiles without modification.
2. **SSR safety:** `"use client"` directive preserved (line 1).
3. **LAW II honest fallback:** vega-embed catch now triggers explicit visible error pane instead of silent console.error.
4. **Cancellation guard:** `setError` only fires when `!cancelled` — no post-unmount state update.
5. **Retry-friendly:** mount div is always rendered (sibling to error pane), so future `spec` changes re-trigger `useEffect` and can recover.
6. **Vega path mark assertion:** rect marks render as SVG `<path>` (per Codex iter-1 P1 + vega-scenegraph SVGRenderer source). Spec asserts `svg path` count > 0, not `<rect>`.
7. **§9.4 N/A frontend.**
8. **CHARTER §1 LOC cap:** 93 net. Under 200.
9. **No new npm dependency:** vega-embed already in package.json.

   1: "use client";
   2: 
   3: import vegaEmbed from "vega-embed";
   4: import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
   5: 
   6: import type { VegaLiteSpec } from "@/lib/api";
   7: 
   8: interface VegaChartProps {
   9:   spec: VegaLiteSpec;
  10:   className?: string;
  11:   onPointClick?: (datum: Record<string, unknown>) => void;
  12: }
  13: 
  14: /**
  15:  * F10 Vega-Lite v5 client renderer (Phase 2B Task 2B.2 frontend half).
  16:  *
  17:  * Renders a Vega-Lite spec via vega-embed. The spec arrives from the
  18:  * backend `/runs/{run_id}/charts/{chart_type}` endpoint with the
  19:  * polaris_provenance extension. Click events on datums fire onPointClick
  20:  * with the datum (which includes evidence_id) so the host page can
  21:  * surface the source span.
  22:  *
  23:  * I-f10-001: surfaces vega-embed errors in an explicit `data-testid="vega-chart-error"`
  24:  * pane (LAW II — fail loudly, no silent empty chart). Mount div remains
  25:  * present so future spec changes can re-trigger the embed.
  26:  */
  27: export function VegaChart({ spec, className, onPointClick }: VegaChartProps) {
  28:   const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
  29:   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  30: 
  31:   useEffect(() => {
  32:     if (!ref.current) return;
  33:     let cancelled = false;
  34:     let viewToFinalize: { finalize: () => void } | null = null;
  35: 
  36:     setError(null);
  37: 
  38:     // VegaLiteSpec from our API types is intentionally permissive; vega-embed
  39:     // narrows to its full TopLevelSpec type. Casting through unknown is the
  40:     // documented bridge.
  41:     vegaEmbed(ref.current, spec as unknown as Parameters<typeof vegaEmbed>[1], {
  42:       actions: false,
  43:       renderer: "svg",
  44:     })
  45:       .then((result) => {
  46:         if (cancelled) {
  47:           result.view.finalize();
  48:           return;
  49:         }
  50:         viewToFinalize = result.view;
  51:         if (onPointClick) {
  52:           result.view.addEventListener("click", (_event, item) => {
  53:             if (item?.datum) {
  54:               onPointClick(item.datum as Record<string, unknown>);
  55:             }
  56:           });
  57:         }
  58:       })
  59:       .catch((err) => {
  60:         console.error("vega-embed render failed", err);
  61:         if (!cancelled) {
  62:           setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
  63:         }
  64:       });
  65: 
  66:     return () => {
  67:       cancelled = true;
  68:       viewToFinalize?.finalize();
  69:     };
  70:   }, [spec, onPointClick]);
  71: 
  72:   return (
  73:     <>
  74:       {error !== null ? (
  75:         <div
  76:           data-testid="vega-chart-error"
  77:           role="alert"
  78:           className="rounded border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/5 p-3 text-xs text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
  79:         >
  80:           Vega-Lite render failed: {error}
  81:         </div>
  82:       ) : null}
  83:       <div
  84:         ref={ref}
  85:         data-testid="vega-chart"
  86:         className={className ?? "polaris-vega-chart w-full overflow-x-auto"}
  87:       />
  88:     </>
  89:   );
  90: }

 611: function ChartsTab({
 612:   runId,
 613:   onSelect,
 614: }: {
 615:   runId: string;
 616:   onSelect: (id: string) => void;
 617: }) {
 618:   const [chartType, setChartType] = useState<ChartType>("forest_plot");
 619:   const [spec, setSpec] = useState<VegaLiteSpec | null>(null);
 620:   const [chartError, setChartError] = useState<string | null>(null);
 621: 
 622:   useEffect(() => {
 623:     let cancelled = false;
 624:     getChart(runId, chartType)
 625:       .then((s) => {
 626:         if (!cancelled) {
 627:           setSpec(s);
 628:           setChartError(null);
 629:         }
 630:       })
 631:       .catch((err) => {
 632:         if (!cancelled) {
 633:           setSpec(null);
 634:           setChartError(
 635:             err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Chart load failed",
 636:           );
 637:         }
 638:       });
 639:     return () => {
 640:       cancelled = true;
 641:     };
 642:   }, [runId, chartType]);
 643: 
 644:   const types: ChartType[] = ["forest_plot", "comparison_table", "timeline"];
 645: 
 646:   return (
 647:     <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
 648:       <div className="flex gap-2">
 649:         {types.map((t) => (
 650:           <button
 651:             key={t}
 652:             type="button"

 661:           </button>

 665:         <p

   1: "use client";
   2: 
   3: import vegaEmbed from "vega-embed";
   4: import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
   5: 
   6: import type { VegaLiteSpec } from "@/lib/api";
   7: 
   8: interface VegaChartProps {
   9:   spec: VegaLiteSpec;
  10:   className?: string;
  11:   onPointClick?: (datum: Record<string, unknown>) => void;
  12: }
  13: 
  14: /**
  15:  * F10 Vega-Lite v5 client renderer (Phase 2B Task 2B.2 frontend half).
  16:  *
  17:  * Renders a Vega-Lite spec via vega-embed. The spec arrives from the
  18:  * backend `/runs/{run_id}/charts/{chart_type}` endpoint with the
  19:  * polaris_provenance extension. Click events on datums fire onPointClick
  20:  * with the datum (which includes evidence_id) so the host page can
  21:  * surface the source span.
  22:  *
  23:  * I-f10-001: surfaces vega-embed errors in an explicit `data-testid="vega-chart-error"`
  24:  * pane (LAW II — fail loudly, no silent empty chart). Mount div remains
  25:  * present so future spec changes can re-trigger the embed.
  26:  */
  27: export function VegaChart({ spec, className, onPointClick }: VegaChartProps) {
  28:   const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);
  29:   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  30: 
  31:   useEffect(() => {
  32:     if (!ref.current) return;
  33:     let cancelled = false;
  34:     let viewToFinalize: { finalize: () => void } | null = null;
  35: 
  36:     setError(null);
  37: 
  38:     // VegaLiteSpec from our API types is intentionally permissive; vega-embed
  39:     // narrows to its full TopLevelSpec type. Casting through unknown is the
  40:     // documented bridge.
  41:     vegaEmbed(ref.current, spec as unknown as Parameters<typeof vegaEmbed>[1], {
  42:       actions: false,
  43:       renderer: "svg",
  44:     })
  45:       .then((result) => {
  46:         if (cancelled) {
  47:           result.view.finalize();
  48:           return;
  49:         }
  50:         viewToFinalize = result.view;
  51:         if (onPointClick) {
  52:           result.view.addEventListener("click", (_event, item) => {
  53:             if (item?.datum) {
  54:               onPointClick(item.datum as Record<string, unknown>);
  55:             }
  56:           });
  57:         }
  58:       })
  59:       .catch((err) => {
  60:         console.error("vega-embed render failed", err);
  61:         if (!cancelled) {
  62:           setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
  63:         }
  64:       });
  65: 
  66:     return () => {
  67:       cancelled = true;
  68:       viewToFinalize?.finalize();
  69:     };
  70:   }, [spec, onPointClick]);
  71: 
  72:   return (
  73:     <>
  74:       {error !== null ? (
  75:         <div
  76:           data-testid="vega-chart-error"
  77:           role="alert"
  78:           className="rounded border border-rose-500/40 bg-rose-500/5 p-3 text-xs text-rose-700 dark:text-rose-300"
  79:         >
  80:           Vega-Lite render failed: {error}
  81:         </div>
  82:       ) : null}
  83:       <div
  84:         ref={ref}
  85:         data-testid="vega-chart"
  86:         className={className ?? "polaris-vega-chart w-full overflow-x-auto"}
  87:       />
  88:     </>
  89:   );
  90: }

This consolidates instead of forking the renderer (Codex iter-1 P2).
.codex\I-f10-001\brief.md:19:- **P2 fix (width/height):** existing API has no width/height props — width/height should be expressed in the **Vega-Lite spec** itself (`width: 600, height: 300` top-level fields), which is the canonical Vega-Lite way. Drop the props from the new API; the demo spec sets them inline.
.codex\I-f10-001\brief.md:20:- **P2 fix (silent fallback per LAW II):** existing `.catch((err) => { console.error(err) })` is a silent fallback (LAW II violation — fail loudly). Iter 2 plan: add `error: string | null` React state; on catch, `setError(err.message)`; render `<div data-testid="vega-chart-error" role="alert">Vega-Lite render failed: {error}</div>` instead of empty mount div.
.codex\I-f10-001\brief.md:37:- **Issue:** I-f10-001 — Vega-Lite renderer (per breakdown text "react-vega + Vega-Lite v5"; scope: "wire react-vega"; acceptance: "sample chart renders"; LOC estimate 120).
.codex\I-f10-001\brief.md:38:- **Substrate:** `vega-embed: ^7.1.0` is ALREADY in `web/package.json` dependencies. Vega-embed is the official upstream library that takes a Vega-Lite v5 spec + a DOM element and renders the chart. **react-vega is a wrapper around vega/vega-lite that we can avoid in favour of vega-embed-direct mounting via a `useRef` + `useEffect`** — this saves the dep cost and keeps bundle size down. The issue title's "react-vega + Vega-Lite v5" describes upstream tooling intent; the acceptance criterion ("sample chart renders") is satisfied by either path. Vega-Lite v5 specs work with vega-embed transparently.
.codex\I-f10-001\brief.md:51:   - In the render JSX: render `<div data-testid="vega-chart">` (mount target, ALWAYS present so future `useEffect` can re-mount) with the error pane rendered as a SIBLING above it: `{error !== null && <div data-testid="vega-chart-error" role="alert" className="...">Vega-Lite render failed: {error}</div>}`. Keeping the mount div present per Codex iter-2 P2.

Drop the props from the new API; the demo spec sets them inline.
.codex\I-f10-001\codex_brief_verdict_iter3.txt:28:- **P2 fix (silent fallback per LAW II):** existing `.catch((err) => { console.error(err) })` is a silent fallback (LAW II violation — fail loudly). Iter 2 plan: add `error: string | null` React state; on catch, `setError(err.message)`; render `<div data-testid="vega-chart-error" role="alert">Vega-Lite render failed: {error}</div>` instead of empty mount div.
.codex\I-f10-001\codex_brief_verdict_iter3.txt:45:- **Issue:** I-f10-001 — Vega-Lite renderer (per breakdown text "react-vega + Vega-Lite v5"; scope: "wire react-vega"; acceptance: "sample chart renders"; LOC estimate 120).
.codex\I-f10-001\codex_brief_verdict_iter3.txt:46:- **Substrate:** `vega-embed: ^7.1.0` is ALREADY in `web/package.json` dependencies. Vega-embed is the official upstream library that takes a Vega-Lite v5 spec + a DOM element and renders the chart. **react-vega is a wrapper around vega/vega-lite that we can avoid in favour of vega-embed-direct mounting via a `useRef` + `useEffect`** — this saves the dep cost and keeps bundle size down. The issue title's "react-vega + Vega-Lite v5" describes upstream tooling intent; the acceptance criterion ("sample chart renders") is satisfied by either path. Vega-Lite v5 specs work with vega-embed transparently.
.codex\I-f10-001\codex_brief_verdict_iter3.txt:59:   - In the render JSX: render `<div data-testid="vega-chart">` (mount target, ALWAYS present so future `useEffect` can re-mount) with the error pane rendered as a SIBLING above it: `{error !== null && <div data-testid="vega-chart-error" role="alert" className="...">Vega-Lite render failed: {error}</div>}`. Keeping the mount div present per Codex iter-2 P2.

@@ -0,0 +1,23 @@
+import { expect, test } from "@playwright/test";
+
+test("Charts test route renders the Vega-Lite v5 sample bar chart", async ({
+  page,
+}) => {
+  await page.goto("/charts_test");
+
+  const chart = page.getByTestId("vega-chart");
+  await expect(chart).toBeVisible();
+
+  // vega-embed uses { renderer: "svg" } so the chart content is an SVG root.
+  const svg = chart.locator("svg");
+  await expect(svg.first()).toBeVisible({ timeout: 10_000 });
+
+  // Vega rect (bar) marks render as <path> elements (vega-scenegraph
+  // SVGRenderer maps `rect` mark to SVG `path`). Three demo data points →
+  // at least three mark <path> elements.
+  const paths = chart.locator("svg path");
+  expect(await paths.count()).toBeGreaterThan(0);
+
+  // No error pane should render on a valid spec.
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("vega-chart-error")).toHaveCount(0);
+});

## What changed

### `vega-chart.tsx` (production)
- Added `useState<string | null>` for `error`.
- `setError(null)` at start of each `useEffect` invocation (clear stale; per Codex iter-2 P2).
- `.catch` block now calls `setError(...)` only when `!cancelled` (avoid post-unmount state update).
- Render a sibling `<div data-testid="vega-chart-error" role="alert">` ABOVE the mount div when `error !== null`. Mount div remains permanently in JSX so future spec changes can re-trigger embed.
- Added `data-testid="vega-chart"` to mount div for Playwright.
- Existing API (`spec`, `className`, `onPointClick`) preserved unchanged → existing inspector consumer at `web/app/inspector/[runId]/page.tsx` continues to work without source modification.

### `charts_test/page.tsx` (NEW demo route)
- Hand-authored Vega-Lite v5 sample spec: `$schema` v5 URL; bar chart of 3 data points (POLARIS / ChatGPT DR / Gemini DR scores on "Sourcing" dimension); `width`/`height` set in spec; `polaris_provenance: { chart_type: "forest_plot", evidence_ids: ["demo-1","demo-2","demo-3"] }` (per `VegaLiteSpec` contract; "forest_plot" is one of the 3 valid `ChartType` values).
- Honest-frame copy explains "demo evidence_ids only; consumed by real forest-plot in I-f10-002."

### `vega_lite_chart.spec.ts` (Playwright)
- Visit `/charts_test`, assert `[data-testid="vega-chart"]` visible, wait for `svg` to attach (≤10s), assert `svg path` count > 0 (Vega rect marks are SVG paths per Codex iter-1 P1 verification), assert no `[data-testid="vega-chart-error"]`.

  30: 
  31:     // VegaLiteSpec from our API types is intentionally permissive; vega-embed
  32:     // narrows to its full TopLevelSpec type. Casting through unknown is the
  33:     // documented bridge.
  34:     vegaEmbed(ref.current, spec as unknown as Parameters<typeof vegaEmbed>[1], {
  35:       actions: false,
  36:       renderer: "svg",
  37:     })
  38:       .then((result) => {
  39:         if (cancelled) {
  40:           result.view.finalize();
  41:           return;
  42:         }
  43:         viewToFinalize = result.view;
  44:         if (onPointClick) {
  45:           result.view.addEventListener("click", (_event, item) => {
  46:             if (item?.datum) {
  47:               onPointClick(item.datum as Record<string, unknown>);
  48:             }
  49:           });
  50:         }
  51:       })
  52:       .catch((err) => {
  53:         console.error("vega-embed render failed", err);
  54:       });
  55: 
  56:     return () => {
  57:       cancelled = true;
  58:       viewToFinalize?.finalize();
  59:     };
  60:   }, [spec, onPointClick]);
  61: 
  62:   return (
  63:     <div
  64:       ref={ref}
  65:       className={className ?? "polaris-vega-chart w-full overflow-x-auto"}
  66:     />
  67:   );
  68: }

Each hash entry (property) uses\n the operation identifiers specified in rfc6902.\n In this way, we can map each patch operation\n to its dedicated function in efficient way.\n */\n/* The operations applicable to an object */\nvar objOps = {\n    add: function (obj, key, document) {\n        obj[key] = this.value;\n        return { newDocument: document };\n    },\n    remove: function (obj, key, document) {\n        var removed = obj[key];\n        delete obj[key];\n        return { newDocument: document, removed: removed };\n    },\n    replace: function (obj, key, document) {\n        var removed = obj[key];\n        obj[key] = this.value;\n        return { newDocument: document, removed: removed };\n    },\n    move: function (obj, key, document) {\n        /* in case move target overwrites an existing value,\n        return the removed value, this can be taxing performance-wise,\n        and is potentially unneeded */\n        var removed = getValueByPointer(document, this.path);\n        if (removed) {\n            removed = _deepClone(removed);\n        }\n        var originalValue = applyOperation(document, { op: \"remove\", path: this.from }).removed;\n        applyOperation(document, { op: \"add\", path: this.path, value: originalValue });\n        return { newDocument: document, removed: removed };\n    },\n    copy: function (obj, key, document) {\n        var valueToCopy = getValueByPointer(document, this.from);\n        // enforce copy by value so further operations don't affect source (see issue #177)\n        applyOperation(document, { op: \"add\", path: this.path, value: _deepClone(valueToCopy) });\n        return { newDocument: document };\n    },\n    test: function (obj, key, document) {\n        return { newDocument: document, test: _areEquals(obj[key], this.value) };\n    },\n    _get: function (obj, key, document) {\n        this.value = obj[key];\n        return { newDocument: document };\n    }\n};\n/* The operations applicable to an array. \"_get\", path: pointer };\n    applyOperation(document, getOriginalDestination);\n    return getOriginalDestination.value;\n}\n/**\n * Apply a single JSON Patch Operation on a JSON document.\n * operation.value;\n            returnValue.removed = document; //document we removed\n            return returnValue;\n        }\n        else if (operation.op === 'move' || operation.op === 'copy') { }\n        }\n    } /* END ROOT OPERATIONS */\n    else {\n        if (!mutateDocument) {\n            document = _deepClone(document);\n        }\n        var path = operation.path || \"\";\n existingPathFragment) {\n    if (typeof operation !== 'object' || operation === null || Array.isArray(operation)) {\n        throw new JsonPatchError('Operation is not an object', 'OPERATION_NOT_AN_OBJECT', index, operation, document);\n    }\n    else if (!objOps[operation.op]) {\n        throw new JsonPatchError('Operation `op` property is not one of operations defined in    }\n        }\n        else if (operation.op === 'replace' || operation.op === 'remove' || operation.op === '_get') {\n            if (operation.path !== existingPathFragment) {\n CONNECTION WITH THE SOFTWARE OR THE USE OR OTHER DEALINGS IN THE\n// SOFTWARE.\nexport function _areEquals(a, b) {\n    if (a === b)\n        return true;\n    if (a && b && typeof a == 'object' && typeof b == 'object') {\n        var arrA = Array.isArray(a), arrB = Array.isArray(b), i, length, key;\n        if (arrA && arrB) {\n            length = a.length;\n            if (length != * (c) 2017-2021 Joachim Wester\n * MIT license\n */\nimport { _deepClone, _objectKeys, escapePathComponent, hasOwnProperty } from './helpers.mjs';\nimport { applyPatch } from './core.mjs';\nvar beforeDict = new WeakMap();\nvar Mirror = /** @class */ (function () {\n    function Mirror(obj) {\n        this.observers = new Map();\n        this.obj = obj;\n    }\n    return Mirror;\n}());\nvar ObserverInfo = /** @class */ (function () {\n    function ObserverInfo(callback, observer) {\n        this.callback = callback;\n        this.observer = observer;\n    }\n    return observer.unobserve();\n}\n/**\n * Observes changes made to an object, which can then be retrieved using generate\n */\nexport function observe(obj, callback) {\n    var patches = [];\n    var observer;\n    var mirror = getMirror(obj);\n    if (!mirror) {\n        mirror = new Mirror(obj);\n        beforeDict.set(obj, mirror);\n    }\n    else {\n        var observerInfo =        window.addEventListener('mouseup', fastCheck);\n            window.addEventListener('keyup', fastCheck);\n            window.addEventListener('mousedown', fastCheck);\n value = this.map.get(key)\n    if (value === undefined) {\n      return undefined\n    } else {\n      // Remove the key from the map and add it to the end\n      this.map.delete(key)\n      this.map.set(key, value)\n      return value\n    }\n  }\n\n  delete (key) {\n    return this.map.delete(key)\n  }\n\n  set (key, value) {\n    const deleted = this.delete(key)\n\n    if (!deleted && value !== undefined) {\n      // If cache is full, delete the least recently used item\n      if (this.map.size >= this.max) {\n        const firstKey = this.map.keys().next().value\n        this.delete(firstKey)\n      }\n\n      this.map.set(key, value)\n    }\n\n    return this\n  }\n}\n\nmodule.exports = LRUCache\n","'use strict'\n\nconst ANY = Symbol('SemVer ANY')\n// hoisted class for cyclic dependency\nclass Comparator {\n  static get ANY () {\n    return ANY\n  }\n\n  constructor (comp, options) {\n    options = parseOptions(options)\n\n    if (comp instanceof Comparator) {\n this.operator = ''\n    }\n\n    // if it literally is just '>' or '' then allow anything.\n    if (!m[2]) {\n      this.semver = ANY\n    } else {\n      this.semver = new SemVer(m[2],    }\n    }\n\n    return cmp(version, this.operator, this.semver, this.options)\n  }\n\n  intersects (comp, options) {\n    if (!(comp instanceof Comparator)) {\n      throw new TypeError('a Comparator is required')\n    }\n\n    if (this.operator === '') {\n      if (this.value === '') {\n        return true\n      }\n      return new Range(comp.value, options).test(this.value)\n    } calculatePositionRelativeToCursor(event, tooltipBox, { offsetX, offsetY }) {\n    // the possible positions for the tooltip\n    const positions = getPositions({ x1: event.clientX, x2: event.clientX, the viewport.\nfunction getMarkBounds(containerBox, origin, item) {\n    // if this is a voronoi mark, we want to use the bounds of the point that voronoi cell represents\n    const markBounds = item.isVoronoi ? item.datum.bounds : item.bounds;\n    let left = containerBox.left + origin[0] + markBounds.x1;\n    let top = containerBox.top + origin[1] + markBounds.y1;\n    // traverse mark  227: /**
 228:  * Embed a Vega visualization component in a web page. This function returns a promise.
 229:  *
 230:  * @param el        DOM element in which to place component (DOM node or CSS selector).
 231:  * @param spec      String : A URL string from which to load the Vega specification.
 232:  *                  Object : The Vega/Vega-Lite specification as a parsed JSON object.
 233:  * @param opts       A JavaScript object containing options for embedding.
 234:  */
 235: export default async function embed(
 236:   el: HTMLElement | string,
 237:   spec: VisualizationSpec | string,
 238:   opts: EmbedOptions = {},
 239: ): Promise<Result> {
 240:   let parsedSpec: VisualizationSpec;
 241:   let loader: Loader | undefined;
 242: 
 243:   if (isString(spec)) {
 244:     loader = createLoader(opts.loader);
 245:     parsedSpec = JSON.parse(await loader.load(spec));
 246:   } else {
 247:     parsedSpec = spec;
 248:   }
 249: 
 250:   const loadedEmbedOptions = embedOptionsFromUsermeta(parsedSpec);
 251:   const usermetaLoader = loadedEmbedOptions.loader;
 252: 
 253:   // either create the loader for the first time or create a new loader if the spec has new loader options
 254:   if (!loader || usermetaLoader) {
 255:     loader = createLoader(opts.loader ?? usermetaLoader);
 256:   }
 257: 
 258:   const usermetaOpts = await loadOpts(loadedEmbedOptions, loader);
 259:   const parsedOpts = await loadOpts(opts, loader);
 260: 
 261:   const mergedOpts = {
 262:     ...mergeDeep(parsedOpts, usermetaOpts),
 263:     config: mergeConfig(parsedOpts.config ?? {}, usermetaOpts.config ?? {}),
 264:   };
 265: 
 266:   return await _embed(el, parsedSpec, mergedOpts, loader);
 267: }
 268: 
 269: async function loadOpts(opt: EmbedOptions, loader: Loader): Promise<EmbedOptions<never>> {
 270:   const config: Config = isString(opt.config) ? JSON.parse(await loader.load(opt.config)) : (opt.config ?? {});
 271:   const patch: PatchFunc | Operation[] = isString(opt.patch) ? JSON.parse(await loader.load(opt.patch)) : opt.patch;
 272:   return {
 273:     ...(opt as any),
 274:     ...(patch ? {patch} : {}),
 275:     ...(config ? {config} : {}),
 276:   };
 277: }
 278: 
 279: function getRoot(el: Element) {
 280:   const possibleRoot = el.getRootNode ? el.getRootNode() : document;
 281:   return possibleRoot instanceof ShadowRoot
 282:     ? {root: possibleRoot, rootContainer: possibleRoot}
 283:     : {root: document, rootContainer: document.head ?? document.body};
 284: }
 285: 
 286: async function _embed(
 287:   el: HTMLElement | string,
 288:   spec: VisualizationSpec,
 289:   opts: EmbedOptions<never> = {},
 290:   loader: Loader,
 291: ): Promise<Result> {
 292:   const config = opts.theme ? mergeConfig(themes[opts.theme], opts.config ?? {}) : opts.config;
 293: 
 294:   const actions = isBoolean(opts.actions) ? opts.actions : mergeDeep<Actions>({}, DEFAULT_ACTIONS, opts.actions ?? {});
 295:   const i18n = {...I18N, ...opts.i18n};
 296: 
 297:   const renderer = opts.renderer ?? 'svg';
 298:   const logger = opts.logger ?? VgLogger(vega.Warn);
 299:   if (opts.logLevel !== undefined) logger.level(opts.logLevel);
 300: 
 301:   const downloadFileName = opts.downloadFileName ?? 'visualization';
 302: 
 303:   const element = typeof el === 'string' ? document.querySelector(el) : el;
 304:   if (!element) {
 305:     throw new Error(`${el} does not exist`);
 306:   }
 307: 
 308:   if (opts.defaultStyle !== false) {
 309:     const ID = 'vega-embed-style';
 310:     const {root, rootContainer} = getRoot(element);
 311:     if (!root.getElementById(ID)) {
 312:       const style = document.createElement('style');
 313:       style.id = ID;
 314:       style.innerHTML =
 315:         opts.defaultStyle === undefined || opts.defaultStyle === true
 316:           ? (embedStyle ?? '').toString()
 317:           : opts.defaultStyle;
 318:       rootContainer.appendChild(style);
 319:     }
 320:   }
 321: 
 322:   const mode = guessMode(spec, logger, opts.mode);
 323: 
 324:   let vgSpec: VgSpec = PREPROCESSOR[mode](spec, logger, config);
 325: 
 326:   if (mode === 'vega-lite') {
 327:     if (vgSpec.$schema) {
 328:       const parsed = schemaParser(vgSpec.$schema);
 329: 
 330:       if (!satisfies(VERSION.vega, `^${parsed.version.slice(1)}`)) {
 331:         logger.warn(`The compiled spec uses Vega ${parsed.version}, but current version is v${VERSION.vega}.`);
 332:       }
 333:     }
 334:   }
 335: 
 336:   element.classList.add('vega-embed');
 337:   if (actions) {
 338:     element.classList.add('has-actions');
 339:   }
 340:   element.innerHTML = ''; // clear container
 341: 
 342:   let container = element;
 343:   if (actions) {
 344:     const chartWrapper = document.createElement('div');
 345:     chartWrapper.classList.add(CHART_WRAPPER_CLASS);
 346:     element.appendChild(chartWrapper);
 347:     container = chartWrapper;
 348:   }
 349: 
 350:   const patch = opts.patch;
 351:   if (patch) {
 352:     vgSpec = patch instanceof Function ? patch(vgSpec) : applyPatch(vgSpec, patch, true, false).newDocument;
 353:   }
 354: 
 355:   // Set locale. Note that this is a global setting.
 356:   if (opts.formatLocale) {
 357:     vega.formatLocale(opts.formatLocale);
 358:   }
 359: 
 360:   if (opts.timeFormatLocale) {
 361:     vega.timeFormatLocale(opts.timeFormatLocale);
 362:   }
 363: 
 364:   // Set custom expression functions
 365:   if (opts.expressionFunctions) {
 366:     for (const name in opts.expressionFunctions) {
 367:       const expressionFunction = opts.expressionFunctions[name];
 368:       if ('fn' in expressionFunction) {
 369:         vega.expressionFunction(name, expressionFunction.fn, expressionFunction['visitor']);
 370:       } else if (expressionFunction instanceof Function) {
 371:         vega.expressionFunction(name, expressionFunction);
 372:       }
 373:     }
 374:   }
 375: 
 376:   const {ast} = opts;
 377: 
 378:   // Do not apply the config to Vega when we have already applied it to Vega-Lite.
 379:   // This call may throw an Error if parsing fails.
 380:   const runtime = vega.parse(vgSpec, mode === 'vega-lite' ? {} : (config as VgConfig), {ast});
 381: 
 382:   const view = new (opts.viewClass || vega.View)(runtime, {
 383:     loader,
 384:     logger,
 385:     renderer,
 386:     ...(ast ? {expr: (vega as any).expressionInterpreter ?? opts.expr ?? expressionInterpreter} : {}),
 387:   });
 388: 
 389:   view.addSignalListener('autosize', (_, autosize: Exclude<AutoSize, string>) => {
 390:     const {type} = autosize;
 391:     if (type == 'fit-x') {
 392:       container.classList.add('fit-x');
 393:       container.classList.remove('fit-y');
 394:     } else if (type == 'fit-y') {
 395:       container.classList.remove('fit-x');
 396:       container.classList.add('fit-y');
 397:     } else if (type == 'fit') {
 398:       container.classList.add('fit-x', 'fit-y');
 399:     } else {
 400:       container.classList.remove('fit-x', 'fit-y');
 401:     }
 402:   });
 403: 
 404:   if (opts.tooltip !== false) {
 405:     const {loader: loader_, tooltip} = opts;
 406:     const baseURL = loader_ && !isLoader(loader_) ? loader_?.baseURL : undefined;
 407:     const handler = isTooltipHandler(tooltip)
 408:       ? tooltip
 409:       : // user provided boolean true or tooltip options
 410:         new Handler({baseURL, ...(tooltip === true ? {} : tooltip)}).call;
